01.3 Button Lab¶

This is the basic building blocks for the Python Tkinter window.

  • Contents:

    1. Google Slides Link

    2. Repl.it Link

    3. Lab Overview - What is required.

      a. GUI Solution - This is what the final outcome should look like.

      b. READ.ME File - This is the objectives and rubric.

      c. Build.ME file- This is the code needed to complete the lab.

This lab and Google Slides covers the following content:

  • Syntax for defining a window
  • Tkinter Library import
  • Tk() class instance
  • .geometry method
  • .title method
  • .mainloop method

c. The 'Build.ME' File¶

This file includes all the code necessary to get the lab up and running. It is divided into important sections.¶

In [ ]:
# Objectives.
#   1. Ensure basic window works.
#   2. Add code and run each example 1-4.
#       a. Button basic
#       b. Button attributes (font, relief)
#       c. Multiple Buttons, attribute (command)
#       b. Multiple Buttons attributes (pady, activeforeground, activebackground) and .pack() method.

"""  # Example 1.  Button

myButton = Button(root, text="Button-1")
myButton.pack() 

"""




"""  # Example 2  Font, relief    

myButton = Button(root, text="Button-2", fg = "red", font = "Verdana 14 underline", bd = 2, bg = "light blue", relief = "groove")
myButton.pack()
myButton.pack()

"""




"""   # Example 3 Multiple Buttons, Command to exit


myButton_3 = Button(root, text="Button 3", fg = "yellow", font="Times", bd = 2, bg="purple", relief = "groove")
myButton_3.pack()

myButton_4 = Button(root, text="Button 4", fg = "red", font="Times", bd = 2, bg="gray", relief = "sunken", command=root.destroy)
myButton_4.pack()

"""




""" #  Example 4: Multiple buttons placed around Window

myButton_5 = Button(root, text="5-Purple", activeforeground="yellow", activebackground="purple", font="Times", pady=10)
myButton_5.pack(side=LEFT)

myButton_6 = Button(root, text="6-Blue", activeforeground="yellow", activebackground="blue", font="Times", pady=10)
myButton_6.pack(side=RIGHT)

myButton_7 = Button(root, text="7-Green", activeforeground="orange", activebackground="green", font="Times", pady=10)
myButton_7.pack(side=TOP)

myButton_8 = Button(root, text="8-Red", activeforeground="yellow", activebackground="red", font="Times", pady=10, command=root.destroy)
myButton_8.pack(side=BOTTOM)
